# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="0c29b-104">Types obsolètes dans le .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0c29b-104">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="0c29b-105">Les tableaux de cet article listent les types obsolètes dans .NET Framework 4.5 et .NET Framework 4.6, organisés par assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0c29b-105">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and the .NET Framework 4.6, organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0c29b-106">Utilisez les liens suivants pour consulter la liste des types obsolètes et des alternatives recommandées dans chaque assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0c29b-106">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0c29b-107">Ces types étant obsolètes, tous leurs membres le sont également.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0c29b-107">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0c29b-108">Pour obtenir la liste des membres obsolètes supplémentaires dans la bibliothèque de classes .NET Framework, consultez [Membres obsolètes](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0c29b-108">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>
